DETECTOR   (SOLST) Four solid state detectors suspended from a    F105300500004 
           movable support allowed data to be collected           F105300500005 
           simultaneously at four angles. A fifth solid state     F105300500006 
           detector was held fixed at 90 degr. to the beam        F105300500007 
           direction for use as a monitor during measurement of   F105300500008 
           the angular distributions and as a fifth detector      F105300500009 
           during the measurement of the yield curves.            F105300500010 
SAMPLE     The targets consisted entirely of calcium hydroxide    F105300500011 
           [Ca(OH)2], produced by the rapid reaction of calcium   F105300500012 
           oxide (CaO) with air borne moisture. The angular       F105300500013 
           distributions were measured with targets in which the  F105300500014 
           48Ca enrichment was 87%. The target was estimated to beF105300500015 
           about 3 keV thick.                                     F105300500016 
METHOD     (BCINT)                                                F105300500017

           normalization was estimated to be 10% due to possible  F105300500019 
           systematic errors arising from target nonuniformity,   F105300500020 
           charge collection, and uncertainty as to the chemical  F105300500021 
           nature of the target. Of this total approximately 5%   F105300500022 
           was due to statistical errors in the data.             F105300500023
